103â†’  contextVars: z.record(z.union([z.string(), z.number(), z.boolean(), z.object({}), z.null()])).optional(),\n   104â†’});\n   105â†’export type AiStageExecutionInput = z.infer<typeof   })).optional(),\n   137â†’    groundingSupports: z.array(z.object({\n   138â†’      segment: z.object({\n   139â†’        startIndex: z.number().optional(),\n   140â†’        endIndex: z.number(),\n }).optional(),\n   171â†’  usageMetadata: z.object({\n   172â†’    thoughtsTokenCount: z.number().optional(),\n   173â†’    candidatesTokenCount: z.number().optional(),\n   174â†’    totalTokenCount: }\n   349â†’    \n   350â†’    const shouldEnableUrlContext = \n   351â†’      groundingSettings?.urlContext?.enabled && \n   352â†’      urlsToProcess.length > 0;\n   353â†’\n   354â†’    // 384â†’\n   385â†’    // ðŸš€ NEW: Use direct Gemini API for Google Search grounding (bypassing Genkit)\n   386â†’    if (shouldEnableGoogleSearch || shouldEnableUrlContext) {\n   387â†’ Firebase compatibility\n   782â†’   */\n   783â†’  private cleanUndefinedValues(obj: any): any {\n   784â†’    if (obj === null || obj === undefined) {\n   785â†’      return null;\n   786â†’    }\n   787â†’\n   788â†’    // Handle functions (Firebase doesn't accept functions)\n   789â†’    if (typeof obj === 'function') {\n   790â†’      console.warn('[DocumentPersistence] Function detected in data, converting to null');\n   791â†’      return null;\n   792â†’    }\n   793â†’\n   794â†’    // Handle Dates (convert to ISO string for Firebase)\n   795â†’    if (obj instanceof Date) {\n      // Check for circular references or DOM nodes\n   807â†’      try {\n   808â†’        JSON.stringify(obj);\n   809â†’      } catch (e) {\n   810â†’        console.warn('[DocumentPersistence] Non-serializable object detected, converting to string representation', e);\n   811â†’        return String(obj);\n   812â†’      }\n   813â†’\n   814â†’      // Handle specific known problematic types\n   815â†’      if (obj instanceof File || obj instanceof Blob) {\n   816â†’        console.warn('[DocumentPersistence] File/Blob detected, converting to metadata');\n   817â†’        return {\n   818â†’          type: 'file',\n   819â†’          name: obj instanceof File ? obj.name : 'unnamed',\n   820â†’          size: obj.size,\n   821â†’          mimeType: obj.type\n   822â†’        };\n   823â†’      }\n   824â†’\n   825â†’      // Handle ArrayBuffer and typed arrays\n   826â†’      if (obj instanceof ArrayBuffer || ArrayBuffer.isView(obj)) {\n   827â†’        console.warn('[DocumentPersistence] ArrayBuffer detected, converting to null');\n   828â†’        return null;\n   829â†’      }\n   830â†’\n   831â†’      // Handle Map objects\n   832â†’      if (obj instanceof Map) {\n   833â†’        console.warn('[DocumentPersistence] Map detected, converting to plain object');\n   834â†’        const mapObj: any = {};\n   835â†’        obj.forEach((value, key) => {\n   836â†’          mapObj[String(key)] = this.cleanUndefinedValues(value);\n   837â†’        });\n   838â†’        return mapObj;\n   839â†’      }\n   840â†’\n   841â†’      // Handle Set objects\n   842â†’      if (obj instanceof Set) {\n   843â†’        console.warn('[DocumentPersistence] Set detected, converting to array');\n   844â†’        return Array.from(obj).map(item => this.cleanUndefinedValues(item));\n   845â†’      }\n   846â†’\n   847â†’      // Handle Error objects\n   848â†’      if (obj instanceof Error) {\n   849â†’        return {\n   850â†’          name: cause Firestore issues\n   857â†’      const cleaned: any = {};\n   858â†’      for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {\n   859â†’        // Skip undefined values and functions\n   860â†’        if (value !== undefined && typeof value !== 'function') {\n   861â†’          // Also skip keys that start with underscore (often internal properties)\n   862â†’          if (!key.startsWith('_')) {\n   863â†’            const cleanedValue = this.cleanUndefinedValues(value);\n   864â†’            // Only add non-null, non-undefined values\n   865â†’            if (cleanedValue !== null && cleanedValue !== undefined) {\n   866â†’              cleaned[key] = cleanedValue;\n   867â†’            }\n   868â†’          }\n   869â†’        }\n   870â†’      }\n   871â†’      return cleaned;\n   872â†’    }\n   873â†’\n   874â†’    // Handle primitive values\n   875â†’    return obj;\n   876â†’  }\n   877â†’\n   878â†’  /**\n   879â†’   * Calculate word count from stage outputs\n   880â†’   */\n   881â†’  private calculateWordCount(stageStates: Record<string, StageState>): number {\n   882â†’    let totalWords = 0;\n   883â†’\n   884â†’    Object.values(stageStates).forEach(state => {\n   885â†’      if (state.output && typeof state.output === 'string') {\n   886â†’        totalWords += state.output.split(/\\s+/).filter(word => word.length > 0).length;\n   887â†’      }\n   888â†’    });\n   889â†’\n   890â†’    return totalWords;\n   891â†’  }\n   892â†’\n   893â†’  /**\n   894â†’   * Check if an object has deep nesting (more than 2 levels)\n   895â†’   */\n   896â†’  private
